## <a name="windows-server-2003-r2-attributes"></a><span data-ttu-id="286b5-456">Attributs Windows Server 2003 R2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="286b5-456">Windows Server 2003 R2 Attributes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="286b5-457">Cette classe contient les attributs suivants pour Windows Server 2003 R2 :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="286b5-457">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2003 R2:</span></span>
